<h1 class="top">Abrasive Brush Accessories</h1>


<div id="product-list-media">
  <img src="https://static.rshughes.com/wm/p/wm-230-230-ww/9f419e3891bf263bbfd836151a762366327b5063.jpg?uf=Abrasive-Brush-Accessories" width="230" height="200" title="Abrasive Brush Accessories" id="pp-main-image">

<div class="pp-extra-media">

<div class="wiki-render"><p class="x-newline">Abrasive brush accessories provide adapters, nuts, flanges and mandrels the work with abrasive brush products to convert, adapt or connect products to tools.   Most products are "for use with" specific abrasive brush products.</p></div>
